***уклон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a> (11263)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uklón</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>inclination, rake</li>
<li>slope, declivity, gradient
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыша.html>кры́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uklón</b> krýši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">slope of the roof</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:трубопровод.html>трубопрово́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>uklón</b> truboprovóda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">pipeline pitch</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">idtí pod <b>uklón</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">go downhill</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>bias
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:школа.html>шко́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:технический.html>техни́ческим</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́ном</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">škóla s texníčeskim <b>uklónom</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">school with a technical bias; technical school</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> deviation <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">heretical belief, especially relative to a prescribed form of Communism</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:левый.html>ле́вый</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:правый.html>пра́вый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lévyj/právyj <b>uklón</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">left-wing/right-wing deviation</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:националистический.html>националисти́ческий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уклон.html>укло́н</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nacionalistíčeskij uklón</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">nationalist deviation</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***уклонение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ние</a> (28341)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">уклони́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uklonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uklonénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>evasion, avoidance; dodge</li>
<li>swerve</li>
<li>digression</li>
<li>deviation</li>
<li>deflexion</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уклониться.html>уклони́ться</a> (11045)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">уклони́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uklonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклониться.html>уклони́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uklonítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклоняться.html>уклоня́ться</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:уклоняться.html>уклоня́ться</a> (10431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">уклоня́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uklonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклоняться.html>уклоня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">uklonjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклониться.html>уклони́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn aside, to dodge</li>
<li>to deviate <i>(from a direction)</i></li>
<li>to avoid, to dodge, to evade, to elude</li>
<li>to digress, to wander away</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">уклоня́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">uklonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уклонение.html>уклоне́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uklonénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">уклони́ст</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukloníst</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***укол.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укол.html>уко́л</a> (6005)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укол.html>уко́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukól</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укол.html>уко́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укол.html>уко́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укол.html>уко́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>prick, pricking</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">fencing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hit, touch</li>
<li>injection, shot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:укол.html>уко́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пенициллин.html>пеницилли́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ukól</b> penicillína</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a shot of penicillin</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лать</a> кому́-либо <b><a href = vnd.unilang:укол.html>уко́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">délatʹ/sdélatʹ komú-libo <b>ukól</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give somebody an injection</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>piquing remark, provoking remark</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коло́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">комплектова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">komplektovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укорачивавший.html>укора́чивавший</a> (30930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укорачивавший.html>укора́чивавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukoráčivavšij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укорачивать.html>укора́чивающий</a> (30930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укорачивать.html>укора́чивающий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukoráčivajuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укорачивать.html>укора́чивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukoráčivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укоризна.html>укори́зна</a> (16113)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укоризна.html>укори́зна</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukorízna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укоризна.html>укори́зны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укоризна.html>укори́зны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укоризна.html>укори́зн</a></b>)

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укоризненный.html>укори́зненный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ukoríznennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:безукоризненный.html>безукори́зненный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bezukoríznennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укоризненный.html>укори́зненный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukoríznennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)укори́зненнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)укори́зненней</b>)

***укорять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:укорять.html>укоря́ть</a> (18641)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укор.html>уко́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukór</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reproach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укорять.html>укоря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukorjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:укорить.html>укори́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reproach</li>
<li>to admonish</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***украдкой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:украдкой.html>укра́дкой</a> (8570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:украинский.html>украинском</a></span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мямлить.html>мя́млил</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́л</a>. </span></li>

***украшать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:украшать.html>украша́ть</a> (6553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:украсить.html>укра́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ukrásitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:украшать.html>украша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ukrašátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:украсить.html>укра́сить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to adorn, to embellish, to beautify, to decorate, to ornament</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
